### Round 3: San Marino Grand Prix
*Date: 1991-04-28*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 9: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1991-07-28*

### Round 15: Japanese Grand Prix
*Date: 1991-10-20*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
